And yes, clearly they come from the same "family" of spacecraft... and for the obvious reasons. (</span><span style="font-family: &quot;\22 arial\22 &quot; , &quot;\22 helvetica\22 &quot; , sans-serif;">Does kind-of imply that Hubble itself was a “beard” for a spy satellite program, all along, ah well.)</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;Sure this gift was a good thing! &nbsp;But it also gave NASA a real headache, coming up with an extra half a billion dollars, in order to refit these multi-billion dollar gifts for scientific use.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">What a world.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i>Solve this easily. Vote this year to make America science friendly again. Nothing makes our choice more starkly clear than the <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/gopwaronscience.html">War on Science</a>.</i></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Oh. Lockheed is now doing design work on the <a href="http://www.space.com/32014-human-outpost-near-moon-cislunar-space.html">proposed Cis-Lunar work station</a>, to orbit the Moon and allow studies of both lunar and asteroidal samples, both manned and in autonomous modes.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; This is the right focus and the right goal.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">Sure, not all new space ventures get off the ground. Escape Dynamics sought to do&nbsp;<a href="http://spacenews.com/advanced-space-propulsion-startup-shuts-down/">“external propulsion” using microwave beams</a>&nbsp;to propel a spaceplane to orbit. The theory is very promising. But that apparently wasn’t enough. Well, well. This idea will <i>not</i> go away.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><br /></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><b>== What have we learned recently? ==</b></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">What a universe! &nbsp;A vividly clear, edge-on view of a proto-planetary disk cloud around a young star has raised a real puzzler. While clearly in the process of forming a new planetary system, this belt of dust - looking like a 'flying saucer' - seems to be <a href="http://news.discovery.com/space/astronomy/deep-space-flying-saucer-is-one-cool-planet-forming-disk-160203.htm">far colder than our models say it should be.&nbsp;</a><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Astronomers already know about two sizes of black holes: stellar-mass black holes, formed after the gigantic explosions of very massive stars; and supermassive black holes (SMBH) often found at the centers of galaxies. Now there are signs of </span><a href="http://www.foxnews.com/science/2016/01/15/could-this-be-second-largest-black-hole-in-milky-way.html" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">an intermediate size BH near the giant at our galactic center.</a><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Interesting piece.</span><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Even if it is Fox News… reporting on science.&nbsp;</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="color: #1a1a1a; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://blog.stephenwolfram.com/2016/02/black-hole-tech/" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-V_dnLRMyMGM/VtSPuuYvRsI/AAAAAAAAOig/VvnJrVDuzVM/s320/BLACK-HOLE-TECH.JPG" width="238" /></a></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Stephen Wolfram dabbles dazzlingly into&nbsp;</span><a href="http://blog.stephenwolfram.com/2016/02/black-hole-tech/" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Black Holes and General Relativity</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">I am privileged to know a fair number of people who are way, way smarter than me.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The most luminous galaxy in the Universe - a so-called obscured quasar 12.4 billion light-years away - <a href="http://phys.org/news/2016-01-extreme-turbulence-roiling-luminous-galaxy.html#jCp">is so violently turbulent that it may eventually jettison</a>its entire supply of star-forming gas, according to new observations with the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA).</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">That star, 1800 ly from us, that has experienced a flickering 20% dimming recently roused speculation about “alien megastructures.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">While the astronomers studying it only mentioned it as a lesser possibility, attention sure has been drawn to its behavior, which is unlike any other F-type main sequence star.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Now the fact that it is relatively close by led a researcher to check photos back to 1890,<a href="https://thespacereporter.com/2016/01/alien-megastructure-star-no-longer-explained-comets/"> finding the decline goes that far back, making the “giant comets” explanation seem to decline in probability.</a></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><a href="https://thespacereporter.com/2016/01/alien-megastructure-star-no-longer-explained-comets/">&nbsp;</a> </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">So far, SETI dishes haven’t picked up anything suspicious.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">But the attention speaks well of our civilization, at least some of whose members haven’t forgotten how to be fascinated.</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">In Spanish… <a href="http://www.elespanol.com/ciencia/20160128/97990475_0.html">an article about SETI</a>&nbsp;and the crazy offshoot that wants to send “messages” to ETI. Including comments by yours truly.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Chime in if the Spanish article is good… or bad.</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">A fascinating article describing what we’ve recently learned about the size, shape and stellar types of the&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.dailygalaxy.com/my_weblog/2016/02/the-milky-ways-striking-symmetry-habitable-planets-more-than-5-billion-years-old-closer-to-galaxys-c.html" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">four major spiral arms that make up our Milky Way Galaxy.</a></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Could we spot the signatures of <a href="http://www.space.com/32068-spot-alien-volcanoes-earth-sized-planet.html">large volcanic eruptions</a> in the light-curves from earth-like exoplanets? &nbsp;</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== Within our own Solar System ==</b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.forbes.com/sites/brucedorminey/2016/02/29/nasa-venus-landsail-rover-could-launch-in-2023/#211b31ed5e50" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bLuZ6NxDqPE/VtTUaKSB1tI/AAAAAAAAOjM/7zOQe6MOt9s/s320/Zephyr-1.png" width="320" /></a></div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">In the not-too-distant future, we may sail over the dry surfaces of Venus! <a href="http://www.forbes.com/sites/brucedorminey/2016/02/29/nasa-venus-landsail-rover-could-launch-in-2023/#211b31ed5e50">NASA's Landsail Rover could launch in 2023</a>. The 400 lb "Zephyr" rover has a rigid vertical wing covered with solar sails, and high-temperature electronics designed to withstand the scorching temperatures on the Venusian surface, says lead scientist (and fellow science fiction author) Geoffrey Landis.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">NASA'S New Horizons probe sends back gorgeous&nbsp;photos of the <a href="http://www.nasa.gov/feature/the-frozen-canyons-of-pluto-s-north-pole">frozen canyons of Pluto's&nbsp;north pole region.</a></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">What did we leave behind on the moon? See this <a href="https://anthropoceneacolyte.wordpress.com/2016/02/22/lunar-artifacts-map/">Lunar Artifacts Map</a>, created by Steve Pestana from NASA data.</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Spores in Space! Researchers placed Antarctic deep-rock fungi in 1.4 cm wide cells on a space station platform called EXPOSE-E, which simulated Mars and extreme space conditions.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;A large fraction of the spores&nbsp;<a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/sciencetech/article-3421684/Life-exist-Mars-Antarctic-fungi-survives-Martian-conditions-strapped-outside-space-station.html#ixzz3ybrWlAO3">came active after a year of exposure.&nbsp;</a></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">After a just-completed year in space for astronaut Scott Kelly, here are <a href="http://www.space.com/32071-year-in-space-scott-kelly-7-milestones.html">seven milestones of his time in orbit.</a></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Inspirational!</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">A woman astronaut – an&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Italian space traveler with the European Space Agency – is also a science fiction fan, and she uses this as a&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span class="MsoHyperlink">basis to give a&nbsp;<a href="https://www.blogger.com/goog_1507639459">TEDx talk about what living on the International Space Station is like</a></span></span><a href="https://mail.google.com/mail/u/0/?tab=wm#inbox/152e5e4c16e08077" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">.</a></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">And finally... see t<span style="color: #1d1d1d;">he first official drawing of the <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/02/26/politics/air-force-reveals-image-long-range-strike-bomber-b-21/">U.S. Air Force's B-21 bomber.</a>&nbsp;And yes this is space-pertinent. It used to be our money spent on aerospace black projects would result... maybe once per decade... in taxpayers getting to see something cool that they had paid for. It has now been a very very long time since anything like that has been revealed, even though we <i>know</i>&nbsp;that there have been huge advances in hypersonic and waverider and other super-techs. The excuse has always been the need not to give any help to potential foes, and that's understandable. But the accompanying philosophy has answered: <i>"if adversaries DO know about something, then the American public should know at least that much."</i></span><o:p></o:p></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #1d1d1d;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #1d1d1d;">Come on fellahs and gals. &nbsp;Show us something cooler than a fuzzy artists conception of a super B-2. Make us feel we're the kind of folks building Star Trek. We really need - right now - to feel that way again.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><a href="http://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/extension/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.blogger.com%2Fblogger.g%3FblogID%3D8587336%23editor&amp;media=https%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-V_dnLRMyMGM%2FVtSPuuYvRsI%2FAAAAAAAAOig%2FVvnJrVDuzVM%2Fs320%2FBLACK-HOLE-TECH.JPG&amp;xm=h&amp;xv=sa1.37.01&amp;xuid=0gf8CigKxCzi&amp;description=" style="background-color: transparent; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">“</span><a href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/60-minutes-great-brain-robbery-china-cyber-espionage/"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The Great Brain Robbery”</span></a></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">&nbsp; </span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">was the most highly rated episode of 60 Minutes in seven years, about the systematic use of industrial espionage by China and others, featuring interviews based on the work of international tech-econ guru Mark Anderson, whose <a href="https://www.stratnews.com/">Strategic News Service</a> is vital for you business-newsletter subscribers, and whose </span><i style="font-family: Arial;"><a href="http://www.futureinreview.com/">Future in Review</a>” (FiRe) </i><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">Conference is one of the most important and fun conclaves going</span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">.&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Of course the rapaciously insatiable raid on western inventiveness is a case of killing the goose that lays golden eggs. China's rise has been entirely funded by westerners buying stuff from Asian factories. Just as the same raising-up happened in exactly the same way to Taiwan and Korea, to Japan and postwar Europe and many other zones.</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i>How</i> have Yanks been able to afford 70 years of trade deficits that funded this huge project of uplift? By <i>inventing</i> new industries (rockets, jets, satellites, pharma, telecom, the Internet) to replace old ones we shipped overseas, en masse. Our inventiveness is <i>the</i>&nbsp;key ingredient - after Pax Americana peace - that increased wealth in the world, enlarging a positive-sum pie for all to share.</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Chopping at the neck of that goose proves that Asian elites are no smarter than those of any other pyramidal-hierarchical, command society across 6000 years. &nbsp;Here's a hint. Even if it <i>were</i> a smart move... we won't let it happen.</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== How might the turnaround begin? ==</b></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Not in Asia, I believe. Remember the “Helvetian War” from <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/earth.html">EARTH</a>?<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>It was my forecast (fictional) that the 2020s might feature a consortium of angry&nbsp;<i>developing nations</i> finally getting fed up and declaring hostilities with… Switzerland.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">And other havens for kleptocratic thieves and other cheaters. Cheaters who are the ancient and recurring enemy of not only the poor, but any chance for flat-open-fair-creative capitalism.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>Now see why this flight of science fictional extrapolation is starting to look ever-more likely:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jun/19/tax-havens-money-cayman-islands-jersey-offshore-accounts">Follow the money inside the world's tax havens.</a></span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-juLTKmPpbbM/VrKmQN7EDCI/AAAAAAAAOYM/HnCbMIf_PPQ/s1600/plutocracy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="239" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-juLTKmPpbbM/VrKmQN7EDCI/AAAAAAAAOYM/HnCbMIf_PPQ/s320/plutocracy.jpg" width="320" /></span></a></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">From <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2012/jul/21/offshore-wealth-global-economy-tax-havens?CMP=share_btn_fb">an earlier article in The Guardian</a>: “The world's super-rich have taken advantage of lax tax rules to siphon off at least $21 trillion, and possibly as much as $32tn, from their home countries and hide it abroad – a sum larger than the entire American economy.”&nbsp; According to one expert:</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626;"><i><br /></i></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626;"><i>"If we could figure out how to tax all this offshore wealth without killing the proverbial golden goose, or at least entice its owners to reinvest it back home, this sector of the global underground is easily large enough to make a significant contribution to tax justice, investment and paying the costs of global problems like climate change."&nbsp;</i></span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">To be clear, this is a separate matter from tax rates!<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><b>If you think taxes are too high, you should favor international wealth transparency!</b><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Because tax rates on honest citizens would go <i>down</i>, if all the world's skull-duggerously secreted lucre were announced and tallied.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">I</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">ndeed, work it out. Those trillionaires would then <i>join</i> the fight for low rates, instead of (currently) chortling happily that <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">you</i> are paying for the roads they use and educating their workers and protecting them from revolution.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;\22 arial\22 &quot;;">Nicholas Shaxson discussed this disruption on our economies in his book,&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Treasure-Islands-Uncovering-Offshore-Banking/dp/0230341721/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: '&quot;arial&quot;';">Treasure Islands: Uncovering the Damage of Offshore Banking and Tax Havens</a></span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Treasure-Islands-Uncovering-Offshore-Banking/dp/0230341721/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: '&quot;arial&quot;';">.</a></span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Treasure-Islands-Uncovering-Offshore-Banking/dp/0230341721/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: '&quot;arial&quot;';">&nbsp;</a></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">They count on that service lasting forever. But even&nbsp;if money can stifle modest protest campaigns, like that of Bernie Sanders, in developed nations, there is always the chance of what I described in <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/earth.html">EARTH</a>:&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><br /></i></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i>“<span style="color: #262626;">The struggles of the authorities in Egypt to recover the vast sums hidden abroad by Hosni Mubarak, his family and other cronies during his many years in power have provided a striking recent example of the fact that kleptocratic rulers can use their time to amass immense fortunes while many of their citizens are trapped in poverty. The world's poorest countries, particularly in sub-Saharan </span><span style="text-decoration: none;">Africa</span></i><span style="color: #262626;"><i>, have fought long and hard in recent years to receive debt forgiveness from the international community; but this research suggests that in many cases, if they had been able to draw their richest citizens into the tax net, they could have avoided being dragged into indebtedness in the first place. Oil-rich Nigeria has seen more than $300bn spirited away since 1970, for example, while Ivory Coast has lost $141bn,”</i> notes Heather Stewart in <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2012/jul/21/offshore-wealth-global-economy-tax-havens?CMP=share_btn_fb">The Guardian</a>.&nbsp;</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">How long before some charismatically smart&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">president in some</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;developing nation discovers how much power he/she would have – <i>legally</i> – as a belligerent in an openly and honestly declared <i>state of war </i>against, say, the Cayman Islands?&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Actually look it up, the inherent rights of belligerent states. &nbsp;Rights that - say - the Phillipines could apply to seize - say - Luxembourg or Cayman assets anywhere in the world, without a single shot being fired!</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>What at first might sound ludicrous begins to sound ever-more plausible, the deeper into it you plumb</span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== Theft of our chance to thrive ==</b></span></span></span><br /><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">One of the surest signs of the treason called the War on Science has been the obstinate confederate religious doctrine that we must do </span><i style="color: #262626; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">nothing</i><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> about improving our energy systems. &nbsp;</span><br /><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">If "climate skeptics" had been sincere, they would have said: "</span><i style="color: #262626; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">While </i><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">the jury is out, let's improve efficiency and double research.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">"First: just in case 99% of scientists turn out to be <i>right</i> about the danger.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span></span></span><a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3WGN0Z-kFtY/VtXOZ6HOpKI/AAAAAAAAOj8/zGWKWOWI3Dg/s1600/twoda.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3WGN0Z-kFtY/VtXOZ6HOpKI/AAAAAAAAOj8/zGWKWOWI3Dg/s1600/twoda.jpg" /></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">"But also because efficiency and research are <b><a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2010/07/clarifications-re-climate-skeptics-and.html">TWODA</a></b>&nbsp;-- <b>things we ought to be doing anyway, </b>even if climate change proves false!"</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">That's what sane "skeptics" would have said.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The fact that the Koch-Saudi-financed obstruction campaign <i>never once said those things</i>&nbsp;but instead always&nbsp;<i>sabotaged efficiency and research</i> proves that the goal was always to <i>delay</i> efficiency and alternative energy sources and to sell as much coal and oil as possible, till the world awakened.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">(After auto fuel efficiency standards finally passed in 2009, during the brief democratic Congress, every <i>dire</i> prediction failed and every single <i>positive</i> one came true. &nbsp;We have better, cleaner, smarter, more efficient cars and automakers are selling them very cheap but making profits. Guys, does being wrong EVER change your minds?)</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Now Paul Krugman<a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/02/29/opinion/planet-on-the-ballot.html?_r=1"> weighs in that it's almost game over,</a> amid low gas prices and American energy independence &nbsp;- with Saudi political influence in the U.S. at a 60 year low - tech is accelerating, solar and wind and storage are now competitive and costs are plummeting. Despite treasonous delays, a transformation is pulling away from fossil fuels, faster than anyone imagined possible... and all of it despite the continuing-insane mania and anti-science, anti-future hysteria.</span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Imagine how much sooner and how much better a world, if traitors had not delayed this</span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">.</span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><o:p><b>== Class warfare ==</b></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">I believe one of our problems is that the Rooseveltean reforms – which historians credit with saving western capitalism by vesting the working class with a large stake, (something Marx never expected) – were <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">too successful, </i>in a way. So successful that the very <i>idea</i> of class war seems not even to occur to American boomers. This despite the fact that class conflict was rampant across almost every other nation and time.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>But as boomers age-out, is that grand time of naïve expectation over?<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Forbes recently announced that just 62 ultra-rich individuals have <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/entry/global-wealth-inequality_us_56991defe4b0ce4964242e09?ir=Impact&amp;section=impact&amp;utm_hp_ref=impact">as much wealth as the bottom half of humanity.</a> Five years ago, it took <a href="http://www.forbes.com/sites/chasewithorn/2015/03/02/forbes-billionaires-full-list-of-the-500-richest-people-in-the-world-2015/#2715e4857a0b7575823516e3">388 rich guys</a> to achieve that status. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>Which raises the question, where the heck does this rising, proto-feudal oligarchy think it will all lead?<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">To a restoration of humanity’s normal, aristocratic pyramid of power (with them staying on top)?<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Or to <i>radicalization</i>, as a billion members of the hard-pressed but highly skilled and tech-empowered middle class rediscover class struggle?</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The last time this happened, in the 1930s, lordly owner castes in Germany, Japan, Britain and the U.S. used mass media they owned to stir populist rightwing movements that might help suppress activity on the left. Not one of these efforts succeeded. In Germany and Japan, the monsters they created rose up and took over, leading to immense pain for all and eventual loss of much of that oligarchic wealth.</span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gsvwuadABlk/VrK6-Sd_LgI/AAAAAAAAOYc/Ez5V7Rzf9xg/s1600/capitalism.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="238" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gsvwuadABlk/VrK6-Sd_LgI/AAAAAAAAOYc/Ez5V7Rzf9xg/s320/capitalism.jpg" width="320" /></span></a></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">In Britain and the U.S., 1930s reactionary fomenters dragged us very close to the same path… till moderate reformers did what Marxists deemed impossible – adjusted the wealth imbalance and reduced cheating advantages so that a rational and flat-open-fair capitalism would be moderated by rules and investments to stimulate a burgeoning middle class, without even slightly destroying the Smithian incentives to get rich through delivery of innovative goods and services.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">That brilliant moderation led to the middle class booms of the 50s and 60s and – as I cannot repeat too often - it led to big majorities in our parents’ Greatest Generation adoring one living human above all others: Franklin Delano Roosevelt.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">There are some billionaires who aren’t short-sighted fools, ignorant of the lessons of history.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Bill Gates, Warren Buffet and many tech moguls <i>want wealth disparities brought down </i>through reasonable, negotiated Rooseveltean-style reform that will still leave them standing as very, very wealthy men. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The smart ones know where current trends will otherwise lead. To revolution and confiscation.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>Picture the probabilities,</b> when the world’s poorest realize they could double their net wealth, just by transferring <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">title</i>from 50 men. In that case, amid a standoff between fifty oligarchs and three billion poor, it is the skilled middle and upper-middle classes who’ll be the ones deciding civilization’s course. And who do you think those two billion tech-savvy professionals will side with, when push comes to shove?</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">See my earlier posting:&nbsp;<a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2011/09/class-war-and-lessons-of-history.html">Class War and the Lessons of History.&nbsp;</a></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><o:p><br /></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== Follow the money ==</b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Dark-Money-History-Billionaires-Radical/dp/0385535597/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="clear: right; color: black; float: right; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sex8zNHhd4I/Vpls1s_XRoI/AAAAAAAAOQA/YBCOvJ3xuCs/s1600/dark-money-mayer-koch-brothers.jpeg" /></span></a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Dark-Money-History-Billionaires-Radical/dp/0385535597/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The father of the billionaires Charles G. and David H. Koch&nbsp;<a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/01/12/us/politics/father-of-koch-brothers-helped-build-nazi-oil-refinery-book-says.html?_r=0.">helped construct a major oil refinery in Nazi Germany</a>&nbsp;that was personally approved by Adolf Hitler, according to the just-released &nbsp;"<a href="http://www.amazon.com/Dark-Money-History-Billionaires-Radical/dp/0385535597/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Dark Money: The Hidden History of the Billionaires behind the Rise of the Radical Right,</a>” by Jane Mayer, a new history of the Kochs and other wealthy families whose meddling in U.S. politics and tax loopholes have netted them billions in returns.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Plutocrats-United-Campaign-Distortion-Elections/dp/0300212453/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Of course there is nothing new about feudal lord cheaters. What is new is our slim but real chance of repeating the miracle achieved by our parents in the Greatest Generation... preserving competition and freedom and a flat-open-fair society, despite every effort to warp it, by short-sighted would-be lords.</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-My2-ARUj3tk/Vrfjk3WMzcI/AAAAAAAAObI/52ZhavCGkmM/s1600/41AvCbyWGiL._SX329_BO1%252C204%252C203%252C200_.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-My2-ARUj3tk/Vrfjk3WMzcI/AAAAAAAAObI/52ZhavCGkmM/s320/41AvCbyWGiL._SX329_BO1%252C204%252C203%252C200_.jpg" width="212" /></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">How has money warped the political process? In&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Plutocrats-United-Campaign-Distortion-Elections/dp/0300212453/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Plutocrats United: Campaign Money, the Supreme Court, and the Distortion of American Elections</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">, Richard L. Hasen analyzes the growing importance of campaign financing to modern elections, and</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span><a href="http://ivn.us/2016/01/19/plutocrats-united-impact-citizens-united-isnt-simply-corruption-political-equality/" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">three ways</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">in which money has negatively influenced the democratic process, citing electoral outcomes, legislative influence and eroding public confidence. &nbsp;Hasan proposes reforms -- involving vouchers for citizens to use for campaign contributions and caps on the what a candidate can spend on an election cycle -- that could result in a greater "equality of inputs".&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><br /><br /></div><div class="blogger-post-footer">. . ...a collaborative contrarian product of David Brin, Enlightenment Civilization, obstinate human nature... and http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/ (site feed URL: http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/atom.xml)</div>http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2016/03/international-rivalry-is-much-of-it.htmlnoreply@blogger.com (David Brin)55tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-8587336.post-8050355085993726303Tue, 01 Mar 2016 20:06:00 +00002016-03-01T14:19:24.784-08:00donald trumpgeorge willgun controlsecond amendment Trumpopulists: what will be the priorities?<div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">There is often a logic, beneath shrill jeremiads. For example, Ted Cruz has proclaimed that even one more liberal or moderate justice appointed to the U.S. Supreme Court might shift the reading of the Second Amendment (2A) — does it give private individuals an unlimited right to own guns, or reserve that right only to members of a militia?&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">(Go read the amendment and come back. In Heller v. D.C. the court went with Red America’s wishes by <i>one vote,</i> one interpretative vote. Moreover, let me shudder and add that Cruz is probably right about this one thing. The swing between those two interpretations is very likely to teeter for our lifetimes and more. But in railing about the near-term, he and his followers ignore the long term implication –</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ns4r36QELTU/VtOTr5M1FoI/AAAAAAAAOh0/0bB27dXtDnE/s1600/second-amendment-guns.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="color: black;"><img border="0" height="239" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ns4r36QELTU/VtOTr5M1FoI/AAAAAAAAOh0/0bB27dXtDnE/s320/second-amendment-guns.jpg" width="320" /></span></a></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">-- <i>that the Second Amendment, as currently worded, is by far the weakest in the entire Bill of Rights.</i>&nbsp; If this court or the next one does not reverse Heller, then it will inevitably happen when some huge national tragedy strikes. That’s called the “Ratchet Effect” (see <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/transparentsociety.html">The Transparent Society</a>), and you are behooved to plan, during good times, for what you’ll do at some future crisis, when the public is scared.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">If today's political rightwing were rational, it would be working right now to gather consensus for a <b>new Constitutional Amendment</b> that might protect weapon rights <i>far more firmly </i>than the ambiguous and inherently frail Second. I have <a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2007/01/brin-classics-jefferson-rifle.html">elsewhere</a> described just such an amendment, which could actually pass! Because it offers some needed compromises to liberals and moderates – some positive-sum win-wins - while protecting a core of gun rights more firmly than 2A.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">In fact, this begins a long list of possible compromises that might help left and right wing populists get some of their favorite wishes, while giving up things they deem less important. It used to be called “politics.”&nbsp; Consider trying it, some time.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== My consolation, if Trump gets the GOP nom ==</span></b></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">There are several silver linings to Donald Trump. Oh, I am fretful, for sure. In fact, one of those argent glimmers – that Trump likely <i>does not believe</i> even ten percent of the pandering things that he rants – is as dismaying as it is encouraging.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">One thing is as certain as sunrise. As nominee, he will <a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2016/02/political-battles-in-election-year.html"><i>charge to the center</i> </a>with dazzling, roadrunner agility, leaving it to VP nominee Huckabee or Rubio or even Cruz or some other shrieker to keep the confederates from bolting.&nbsp; As president he would prove both more moderate in policy and vastly more of a sociopathic fibber than even Richard Nixon.&nbsp;</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: black;">Want to know in advance one key moment</span> that could deeply discomfit GOP elders – indeed, that they dread? As nominee, Trump would battle Hillary Clinton or Bernie Sanders very hard. Nastily hard. And yet, at some point in the summer and autumn debates, he is almost certain to say:<i>&nbsp;“Of course the rich pay too little tax!”&nbsp;</i></span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: black;">And thus,</span> with both nominees agreeing, on live TV, that needle would shift, hard. At long last, with almost a consensus sigh, Supply Side Voodoo (SSV) will be finished, precipitating the first of several convergences of left- and right- populisms.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-MOiQ92t5W90/VtOWBeIyf_I/AAAAAAAAOiA/cAj7g9wi5sI/s1600/Trump-emboss.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="color: black;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-MOiQ92t5W90/VtOWBeIyf_I/AAAAAAAAOiA/cAj7g9wi5sI/s320/Trump-emboss.jpg" width="302" /></span></a></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">But the biggest silver lining is simply this.&nbsp; A Trump nomination will <i>make George F. Will’s head explode.&nbsp;</i></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Mr. Will’s <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/opinions/donald-trump-wrecks-the-gop-by-driving-the-campaign-conversation/2016/02/21/b4b6c5b2-d8d4-11e5-925f-1d10062cc82d_story.html">almost-daily rants against Trump</a> are a sight to behold and I confess to gleeful schadenfreude over this bona fide American traitor’s discomfiture. No citizen of this republic was so well placed to denounce and possibly arrest the hijacking of conservatism by monsters, bent on destroying U.S. politics, one of the key problem-solving skills we need, for a fast-changing era. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Will had the intelligence to see that Supply Side was voodoo, utterly disproved by &nbsp;thirty years of diametrically-opposite outcomes. He has known for two decades that the War on Science (and journalism, teaching and all other knowledge castes) was destructive and that the Hastert Rule - against GOP pols ever negotiating in good faith - was outright treason. Faced with the Fox-Limbaugh dumbing-down of American conservatism (financed by oligarchs, many of them foreign, who have no love of Smithian-flat-fair-competititve capitalism), Will at-best occasionally whimpered, then went back to his flack-lackey task of concocting rationalizations for oligarchy.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">This man – this one fellow – could have led a rebellion by conservative intellects to save their movement from Manchurian captivity. It would have been fun! Historically memorable and possibly rewarding… though risky. A real man – and Will has had the nerve to lecture at us, over the years, about manhood – might have accepted the challenge, for the good of his nation and civilization. Indeed, for the good of American conservatism, whose descent into frothing, carpet-chewing hydrophobia can be laid squarely at his feet.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Oh, oh, this will be my solace when I see Donald Trump accepting the Republican nomination. To envision George F. Will swallowing that pill.&nbsp; Reaping the whirlwind that he helped fanatics, foreign meddlers, junkers-lords and quislings to sow. The know-nothing tide and criminally re-ignited civil war that he abetted, using his substantial intelligence to help inflict dogma-rabies upon a nation of pragmatic, problem-solving citizens.</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== Delightful asides ==</b></span><br /><br /><a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/--g-JphfQ40Y/VtX88bvYkPI/AAAAAAAAOkQ/zTGNbTv9_F4/s1600/MADNESS-RIGHT-POLITICS.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="242" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/--g-JphfQ40Y/VtX88bvYkPI/AAAAAAAAOkQ/zTGNbTv9_F4/s320/MADNESS-RIGHT-POLITICS.JPG" width="320" /></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Oh... For those of you calling Marco Rubio the great hope of “moderates” in the Republican Party,&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.forwardprogressives.com/marco-rubio-united-states-governed-god-not-constitution-video/?utm_campaign=shareaholic&amp;utm_medium=facebook&amp;utm_source=socialnetwork" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #0000e9;">have a look at what he says</span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;about “God’s Law always winning over “ even the U.S. Constitution. Those clutching at Sen. Rubio as the </span><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">great hope of Republican "moderates"</i><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> - a man who would throw a 13 year old girl into prison for cleansing herself of any residue, a week after being raped - only show how deep into depravity even Ronald Reagan would call the "moderate" wing of his party.</span><br /><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></i><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">By comparison</i><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">. This&nbsp;</span><a href="http://m.jpost.com/#article=6017RkRFNjQ0MTVEQUI5Mjg2REJDQkU5ODdGRDc0QTE4QjI=" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #0000e9;">stunning piece of rationalization</span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;from a Jordanian journalist asserts that </span><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Saudi Arabia has been devastating Iran,</i><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">crediting a Saudi Prince with ending Iran’s nuclear program and calling low oil prices a deliberate Saudi gambit to crush the Iranian economy.&nbsp;&nbsp;In fact, the article is worth reading! In order to see a weird perspective, and to glimpse some aspects re the War in Yemen of which westerners are mostly-unaware.&nbsp;&nbsp;Still, the entire screed is absurd.&nbsp;&nbsp;Oil price plummets had nothing to do with Iran.&nbsp;&nbsp;That the price drop has cut wages to Shiite radical militias is good, of course, but the end of economic sanctions and ending the drain of a bomb program will both stimulate the main, non-radical elements in Iranian society.&nbsp;&nbsp;Meanwhile, who has the most to dread from Iran rejoining the community of nations, no longer crippled by sanctions?&nbsp;&nbsp;The Saudis, you bet.&nbsp;</span></div><div><br /></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>== Bernie vs Hillary ==</b></span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Okay, Bernie went up one notch in my estimation: Sanders would instigate a <a href="https://berniesanders.com/issues/making-the-wealthy-pay-fair-share/">0.5% tax on stock trades</a> - to reduce speculation and high frequency stock trading.&nbsp; If Congress whittled it in half, that’d be just right. See <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/transactionfee.html">elsewhere</a> my own riffs on why such a transaction tax is utterly essential… including a sci fi reason Bernie won’t mention. I’m still not sure he is my first choice to be president.&nbsp; But boy am I glad he is out there raising lots and lots of policy boldness to our political attention and horizon.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">For the record,</span><span style="color: #0433ff; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span><a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2015/10/hillary-clinton-proposes-financial-transactions-tax.html%EF%BB%BF" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Clinton also supports a transaction tax</a><span style="color: #0433ff; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: black;"><br /></span></span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Sandersites and Hillarites, go ahead and argue.&nbsp; But if you start copying the "passion" and hate we see on the Confederacy side, then we are doomed. <i>Stop it!!</i>&nbsp; Whether Hill or Bern win the nom, they will tell you to replace emotion with iron-willed logic, the way the Union was less frenzied and more logical, when America won vital, earlier phases of this civil war.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br />If Hill wins and you still kinda dislike her?&nbsp; Then <i>turn to a local congressional or state assembly race</i> in which your passion can make a huge, local difference, while grudgingly murmuring "I guess I'll vote for her." And&nbsp; "it's the Supreme Court, stupid."<br /><br />Clinton supporters, make the same vow! Our confederate neighbors are in a science-hating psychosis that is now 100% dogma and 0% facts.&nbsp; Their screeching rage denies all ability to <a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2016/02/the-daggatt-dare-prove-your-pessimism.html">look at ACTUAL OUTCOMES</a> across GOP vs Democratic presidencies.<br /><br />Do... not... be... like... that. We cannot afford it.</span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><b style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">== Your Halloween Costume - plan ahead ==</b></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><br /></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DLVZB2S0USg/VtUtSsS6KNI/AAAAAAAAOjs/7-GNNnDF0wo/s1600/kepi.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="200" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DLVZB2S0USg/VtUtSsS6KNI/AAAAAAAAOjs/7-GNNnDF0wo/s200/kepi.png" width="192" /></a></div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Pay attention to Spike Lee, one of our smartest myth-spinners.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">He gets the power of symbolism, even when only a few percent “get it” consciously.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Take a look at the photo of Spike being interviewed in early 2016.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">His cap is no mere accessory.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">It is a “kepi” worn by Union soldiers during the Civil War.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Four (and also I believe eight) years ago, I urged that folks consider making this their Halloween costume, at minimum, but I was premature.</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Now is the time.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i>(Hey Spike! Come out with your own line of kepis! Offer them for sale!)</i></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">From 1852 till 1865, America suffered horrible betrayals not so much by a region&nbsp;</span><a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2013/02/past-keeping-faith-with-future-and-day.html" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">as a cancerous mindset&nbsp;</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">– feudalist, rancorous, and utterly devoted to romantic oligarchy – rule by plantations lords – for whom a million poor whites willingly fought and suffered and died, striving&nbsp;</span><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">against</i><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;their own best interests. &nbsp;</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">We are now in a later, re-ignited <a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2014/09/phases-of-american-civil-war.html">phase of that same Civil War</a>.&nbsp; And make no mistake, this is not purely regional.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">As Matthew McConaughey’s new movie <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1124037/">“Free State of Jones”</a> will portray, there were many, many believers in the Union and our Great Revolution against feudalism, all across the south.&nbsp; Many of them took up the cause, wearing that blue kepi.&nbsp; I pray that we get through this phase of our Civil War without resort to arms – only a couple of the phases were violent, though all were painful.&nbsp; Elections are best! Still… get the hat.&nbsp;</span></div><div style="line-height: normal; min-height: 14px;"><br /></div><a href="https://www.blogger.com/blogger.g?blogID=8587336" style="background-color: transparent; background-image: url(data:image/png; border: none; cursor: pointer; display: none; height: 20px; opacity: 0.85; position: absolute; width: 40px; z-index: 8675309;"></a><a href="https://www.blogger.com/blogger.g?blogID=8587336" style="background-color: transparent; background-image: url(data:image/png; border: none; cursor: pointer; display: none; height: 20px; opacity: 0.85; position: absolute; width: 40px; z-index: 8675309;"></a><br /><a href="http://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/extension/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.blogger.com%2Fblogger.g%3FblogID%3D8587336%23editor%2Ftarget%3Dpost%3BpostID%3D8050355085993726303%3BonPublishedMenu%3Dposts%3BonClosedMenu%3Dposts%3BpostNum%3D1%3Bsrc%3Dlink&amp;media=https%3A%2F%2F3.bp.blogspot.com%2F-MOiQ92t5W90%2FVtOWBeIyf_I%2FAAAAAAAAOiA%2FcAj7g9wi5sI%2Fs320%2FTrump-emboss.jpg&amp;xm=h&amp;xv=sa1.37.01&amp;xuid=0gf8CigKxCzi&amp;description=" style="background-color: transparent;
