, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #1d1d1d;">The most recent tale in this volume -- <i>"Tumbledowns of Cleapatra Abyss</i>" -- is included in <i>four</i>&nbsp;best-of volumes from 2015, so far, and it's only January.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #1d1d1d;"><br /></span></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #1d1d1d;">Surprises and ironies abound in <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/insistenceofvision.html">Insistence of Vision</a>… as they will in the territory ahead.* Our future. </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 1.75in;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 1.75in;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">More good news?</span><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Download your </span><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">free</i><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">e-version of </span><a href="http://news.microsoft.com/futurevisions/" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">&nbsp;Future Visions:</span></a><span style="color: #1d1d1d; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"> Microsoft has published an anthology of original Science Fiction short stories reflecting&nbsp;its research projects, with entries by Elizabeth Bear, Greg Bear, David Brin, Nancy Kress, Ann Leckie, Robert Sawyer, Seanan McGuire, and Jack McDevitt.&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #1d1d1d; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">My story in Future Visions is the only recent tale of mine that's&nbsp;<i>not</i> </span><span style="color: #1d1d1d; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">included in <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/insistenceofvision.html">Insistence of Vision.</a></span><br /><b style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b><b style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== Star Wars on Trial: the force awakens ==</span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/starwarsontrial.html" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-B3jX9R5MMRQ/VleDJkMI2bI/AAAAAAAAN48/Tn6b9FuS79k/s320/starwarsontrial.jpg" width="213" /></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The new edition of Star Wars on Trial! The new <a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/starwarsontrial.html">“Force Awakens” edition of Star Wars on Trial</a> has been released, just in time to tie in with the Force Awakens movie (Episode -what-is-it-seven?)<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>No, the editions aren't that different. &nbsp;Mostly my new introduction... and a cool modification to the already hilariously apropos cover.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>You still get terrific, incisive, often-sarcastic but also on-target skewerings… and defenses… of this incredibly popular pop-culture phenomenon.&nbsp;</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">And yes... I finally did take the family to see Star Wars: The Force Awakens. See </span><a href="http://davidbrin.blogspot.com/2015/12/jj-abrams-awakens-force.html" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">my comments</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> on this phenomenon.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 1.75in;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 1.75in;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Meanwhile, another author <a href="http://www.vox.com/mischiefs-of-faction/2015/10/9/9486477/jedi-coup-politics">appraises why the Jedi themselves undermined the Old Republic</a>.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>Others are decrypting secrets of Star Wars… as in this <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/StarWars/comments/3qvj6w/theory_jar_jar_binks_was_a_trained_force_user/">hilarious... and rather convincing explanation</a> of how the seemingly insipid and foolish Jar-Jar Binks is almost certainly a Sith master.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>You will chuckle, growl, and finally admit it must be true!</span><br /><b style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b><b style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== Brief looks at recent Sci Fi ==</span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Darkling-Sea-James-L-Cambias/dp/0765336286/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wLeb8FMwp7k/VoxCWYssDGI/AAAAAAAAOLE/WtKkccRw9aU/s320/51bw6wjlGNL._SX327_BO1%252C204%252C203%252C200_.jpg" width="209" /></span></a><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="font-weight: normal;">What alien life might we find under the vast ice shelves of moons such as Jupiter's Europa?&nbsp;</span></span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Darkling-Sea-James-L-Cambias/dp/0765336286/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-weight: normal;">A Darkling Sea</a><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="font-weight: normal;">, by James Cambias, explores a First Contact scenario under the kilometer-thick ice sheet of the moon Ilmatar, which circles a distant gas giant. Humans have established a deep sea research station, with a strict promise of non-interference with the blind, but intelligent creatures that have evolved in the dark ocean depths. Tensions rapidly rise when the Terran crew is discovered, setting the scene for a solid adventure story and complex inter-speces political negotiations... as two vastly different cultures seek to communicate and possibly, reconcile. With intricate world-building&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">and</span><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="font-weight: normal;">&nbsp;vividly detailed aliens.</span></span></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;"><br /></span></span></b></b></span><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cPLLCVFHhPU/VmpVeAkwFrI/AAAAAAAAOBM/fowFvcoSSrc/s1600/the-fold-clines.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cPLLCVFHhPU/VmpVeAkwFrI/AAAAAAAAOBM/fowFvcoSSrc/s320/the-fold-clines.jpg" width="210" /></span></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;">For a fast-paced science fiction mystery-thriller, try&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Fold-Novel-Peter-Clines/dp/0553418297/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-weight: normal;">The Fold</a><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;">, by Peter Clines. The hero, a high school teacher with a perfect eidetic memory and the ability to make tremendous deductive leaps, is called upon to evaluate a super-secret DARPA project -- a team of scientists have developed The Albuquerque Door, a bridge through a fold in space-time. The reclusive researchers claim it works perfectly and will soon be safe for teleporting humans, until things go horrifyingly wrong…</span><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;">&nbsp;with implications that may threaten all of humanity.&nbsp;</span></span></b><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;"><br /></span></span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: #191919; font-weight: normal;">Scheduled for release in January:&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/All-Birds-Charlie-Jane-Anders/dp/1785650556/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-weight: normal;">All the Birds in the Sky</a><span style="color: #191919; font-weight: normal;">, a debut novel from the talented Charlie Jane Anders, editor of io9,&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.sfsignal.com/archives/2015/04/coming-soon-birds-sky-charlie-jane-anders/" style="font-weight: normal;">which SF Signal calls</a><span style="color: #191919; font-weight: normal;">, "a stunning novel about the end of the world - and the beginning of our future.&nbsp;</span></b></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-weight: normal;"><br /></span></span></b></span><a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-RU8dKcIYYEw/VlszJP6eG5I/AAAAAAAAN6k/XxfOZH9iTEQ/s1600/51FUYnijKsL._SX282_BO1%252C204%252C203%252C200_.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="clear: left; color: black; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-RU8dKcIYYEw/VlszJP6eG5I/AAAAAAAAN6k/XxfOZH9iTEQ/s320/51FUYnijKsL._SX282_BO1%252C204%252C203%252C200_.jpg" width="182" /></span></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626;">It’s their planet now! A&nbsp;riveting&nbsp;post-apocalyptic tale that taps into your darkest nightmares: </span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Slavemakers-Joseph-Wallace/dp/0425277186/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Slavemakers<span style="color: #262626;">,</span></a><span style="color: #262626;"> by Joseph Wallace, is a sequel to his earlier novel, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Invasive-Species-Joseph-Wallace-ebook/dp/B00BTRDJNS/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Invasive Species</a>, where deadly parasitic wasps (known as <i>thieves</i>) nearly wipe out humanity. In <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Slavemakers-Joseph-Wallace/dp/0425277186/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Slavemakers</a>, set twenty years later, most remaining humans have been enslaved, under the mind-control of the venomous wasps; &nbsp;isolated pockets of refugees eke out an existence, protected by a vaccine created from a rare cultivated plant. And a few uniquely powerful individuals are able to tap into the linked hive mind of&nbsp;the wasps in order to alter the fate of the planet...</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aB2vYFEpoE4/Vls3XRyyhDI/AAAAAAAAN6w/0tzBhG7VZTA/s1600/word-exhange-graedon.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aB2vYFEpoE4/Vls3XRyyhDI/AAAAAAAAN6w/0tzBhG7VZTA/s320/word-exhange-graedon.jpg" width="207" /></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">What if your tablet&nbsp;didn't just provide you with information, but anticipate your needs, providing prompts... as you find it harder and harder to recall even ordinary words? </span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Word-Exchange-Alena-Graedon/dp/0345806034/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">The Word Exchange</a><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">, a debut novel by Alena Graedon, envisions a near-future where the written word is nearly extinct; people are dependent upon</span><i style="color: #262626;"> </i><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">their handheld </span><i style="color: #262626;">Memes</i><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;to the extent of buying words they can't remember.&nbsp;Our protagonist,&nbsp;Anana Johnson, is assisting her father in producing the final print edition of the </span><i style="color: #262626;">North American Dictionary of&nbsp;the English Language</i><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">, when he mysteriously disappears. She desperately seeks clues, even while communication becomes increasingly challenging as a word flu pandemic sets in, causing many to lose the basic ability to speak. Interesting, but the random word substitutions in the text do slow the flow of the novel.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right: 38.7pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Octavia Butler did a charming short story - <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Wastelands-John-Joseph-Adams/dp/1597801054/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Speech Sounds</a> - along similar lines.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Planetfall-Emma-Newman/dp/0425282392/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-s3evafGbvBU/VmSJMWnxRGI/AAAAAAAAN98/u2mo7WBaFUA/s1600/planetfall-newman.jpeg" /></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">What lies are told to keep society functioning? In Emma Newman’s recent novel,&nbsp;</span><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Planetfall-Emma-Newman/dp/0425282392/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="font-family: Arial;">Planetfall</a><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">, one individual is ‘called’ to an alien planet by a vision. The story takes place twenty-two years after colonists established an outpost at the base of an immense alien artifact -- God’s City. When a mysterious stranger shows up, it opens up long-hidden secrets from the founding of the colony. The story centers around Ren, a talented 3D printing engineer, her social isolation, anxiety, her eventual mental unraveling… and perhaps transcendenc</span></span><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">e.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Keep your eye open, soon, for <b>Avengers of the Moon</b>, a rollicking space opera in the Doc Smith tradition, by Allen Steele, and Charles Stross's new paratime series opener </span><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Dark State</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">.</span></b></span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><br /><div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-right: 38.7pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><br /><span style="font-size: xx-small;">*<span style="font-family: &quot;\22 arial\22 &quot; , &quot;\22 helvetica\22 &quot; , sans-serif;">Which prompts a smile-worthy thought. Our daughter, Ari, observed that “ironman” actually translates as FeMale! A spooky/fey observation and an ironic one… till my wife pointed out that “Fey” and “Irony” are the very same thing. &nbsp;Oog. Never mind that. &nbsp;<a href="http://www.davidbrin.com/insistenceofvision.html">Pre-order <i>Insistence of Vision!&nbsp;</i></a></span></span></div></div></div><a href="http://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/extension/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.blogger.com%2Fblogger.g%3FblogID%3D8587336%23editor%2Ftarget%3Dpost%3BpostID%3D6028930818045959443%3BonPublishedMenu%3Dposts%3BonClosedMenu%3Dposts%3BpostNum%3D1%3Bsrc%3Dlink&amp;media=https%3A%2F%2F1.bp.blogspot.com%2F-aB2vYFEpoE4%2FVls3XRyyhDI%2FAAAAAAAAN6w%2F0tzBhG7VZTA%2Fs320%2Fword-exhange-graedon.jpg&amp;xm=h&amp;xv=sa1.37.01&amp;xuid=0gf8CigKxCzi&amp;description=" style="background-color: transparent; And more science.<div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">I cannot understand the markets’ <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/economy/market-dives-more-than-3-percent-amid-fears-over-oil-prices-china/2016/01/20/010d3a62-bf9f-11e5-bcda-62a36b394160_story.html">panic over lower oil prices</a>.&nbsp; Sure, it hurts if you own Exxon or drilling-fracking services companies, or work for one, or if you are Saudia or Venezuela or Russia or Iran.&nbsp; But for most of the world, it amounts to a spectacular tax cut and cost discount for all manufacturers, transportation and consumers of almost anything. See this article on much <a href="http://www.npr.org/2016/01/20/463724352/as-oil-plummets-cheap-jet-fuel-means-better-travel-deals">cheaper airline deals</a>. <br /><br />&nbsp;Is this flood of spendable cash supposed to somehow… hurt us? For 50 years, steep rises in oil price sent us tumbling into recession and drops helped get us out. &nbsp;What's different this time? &nbsp;Pundits claim that it is because a larger fraction of the oiul we use is produced domestically, now. &nbsp;But (a) that was true in the 1970s too, and the oil shock killed Jimmy Carter. &nbsp;And (b) ...um... increased energy independence from foreign sources is... er,... <i>bad</i>&nbsp;news?</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">&nbsp;plummet in stocks smells funny to me.﻿ I'd look closely at some of those petro state sovereign wealth funds. &nbsp;Just sayin'.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Only now, a truly salient fact that will weave together with the others.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== Does denial have any limits? ==</span></b></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Two U.S. government science agencies announced that 2014, which had smashed the 1998 record as hottest year in human history, did not hold the top title for very long. It’s official, </span><a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/energy-environment/wp/2016/01/20/its-official-2015-smashed-2014s-global-temperature-record-it-wasnt-even-close/" style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">2015 has topped even 2014’s torrid temperatures</a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">.&nbsp; And the forecast is for 2016 to be hotter still.</span><br /><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">But hey, let’s suppose 2016 dips slightly, as would be natural, as each year oscillates around a slope that has arced steadily higher for 50 years. What then? Expect to see Ted Cruz and other murdochians leaping to announce: “See? It’s going DOWN!”&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">(They can no longer use their former lie-trick, pegging the El Nino year 1998 as their “before” comparison. That year, which shattered records across all of recorded human history, was left in the dust by hot 2014 and hotter 2015.)</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">There is only one response… to those of you out there who have bought into the Murdoch-Saudi-Koch-Fox propaganda and War on Science. &nbsp;And I will append that message below.&nbsp;</span></div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== Too late to stop sustainables ==</span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Well, the petro-price plummet might have really hurt us all, if it happened a few years ago, by choking solar and wind companies to death with floods of cheap oil. But it’s too late for that, now.&nbsp;</span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Bloomberg New Energy Finance finds that&nbsp;<a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/energy-environment/wp/2016/01/14/why-clean-energy-is-now-expanding-even-when-fossil-fuels-are-cheap/">2015 was a record year for global investment in the clean energy space</a>, with $329 billion invested in wind, solar panels, biomass plants and more around the world. (The number does not include investments in large hydroelectric facilities).</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wu7F66VQrJo/Vp8kuzSTf2I/AAAAAAAAOSE/3l7QIahBBgg/s1600/CHEAP-OIL.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="238" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wu7F66VQrJo/Vp8kuzSTf2I/AAAAAAAAOSE/3l7QIahBBgg/s320/CHEAP-OIL.JPG" width="320" /></span></a></div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">That’s 3 percent higher than the prior 2011 global investment record of $318 billion — and most striking is that it happened in a year in which key fossil fuels — oil, coal and natural gas — were quite cheap.&nbsp;<i>&nbsp;“</i></span><span style="color: #0e0e0e; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><i>Measured in terms of electricity generating capacity, the world saw an additional 64 gigawatts of wind capacity added and 57 gigawatts of solar capacity, BNEF estimates. The most striking figure here is that while 2015 only saw about 4 percent more clean energy investment than 2014 (when $316 billion was invested), the growth in renewable energy generating capacity was much higher at 30 percent. This, again, signals declining cost.”</i></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><i><br /></i><br />Sure, if oil had dropped five years ago, it would have been a disaster for the Earth by undermining and possibly destroying solar and wind etc. Now? They have huge momentum, are competitive even with&nbsp;<i>cheap</i>&nbsp;oil -- something denialist then claimed to be impossible -- and new techs are looming that will make the transformation epic.<br /><br />At this point,&nbsp;<i>cheap oil is only good news</i>. It frees western nations from fretting to please petro princes, it boosts every industry except corrupt resource extraction, giving both producers and consumers in-effect a huge tax cut (a "tax" that had been going to Saudi Arabia). And it lets us cap the bitumen wells, the tar sand pits and other dirtier sources, reducing fracking, keeping those wells&nbsp;<i>ready</i>&nbsp;in case we need them in-future, a reserve-surge capacity that should keep prices down.&nbsp; Which is exactly the right approach.</span></span><br /><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Energy-World-Flat-Opportunities-Peak/dp/1118868005/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-n1utMce_wBE/Vp8jIF6XCgI/AAAAAAAAOR4/oldgthwffrY/s320/peak-oil.jpg" width="208" /></span></a><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">We lucked out. The princes kept oil high during the span when sustainables were being born. Now the infant is walking and starting to run. And the Carbon Age will taper off, perhaps even in the nick of time. Maybe.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">Oh but timing is everything? Take this headline:<b> Scientists say&nbsp;</b></span><b><a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/energy-environment/wp/2016/01/13/scientists-say-humans-have-basically-canceled-the-next-ice-age/" style="font-family: Arial;">global warming has canceled the next ice age</a>.&nbsp;</b></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">Okay okay. I can just imagine the next denialist chant, after they are forced to move the goal posts yet again. Having to admit that science shows huge global warming due to human-generated CO2? The next riff will be:</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">&nbsp;<i>"Yay!&nbsp; We polluters prevented an inevitable ice age!"&nbsp;</i>&nbsp;</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">That's one interpretation - (a moronic one) - of this scientific study that suggests - indeed - human activity 5000 years ago might have tipped the balance and prevented another glaciation.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br style="font-family: Arial;" /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">In which case&nbsp;<i>yay ancestors.</i>&nbsp;Now let's be scientific and responsible and not wreck the place.</span></span><br /><b style="font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b><b style="font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">== Miscellaneous News Items ==</span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><div class="MsoNormal" style="-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px;"><div style="margin: 0px;"><b style="font-family: Arial;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div></div></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Robert Waldinger heads the 75 year continuous Harvard study of four score men and their families and what traits correlate with long or healthy or happy lives,<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=q-7zAkwAOYg&amp;sns=em">&nbsp;in this fascinating TEDx talk.&nbsp;</a><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><a href="http://xkcd.com/1621/">The Fixion?</a>&nbsp;If they ever find a particle like this one, will they give a Nobel to the XKCD guy, despite his being a cartoonist?&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; So cool.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Dark-Matter-Dinosaurs-Astounding-Interconnectedness/dp/0062328476/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DvO1n57pje0/Vqkksa5UTqI/AAAAAAAAOV8/FZiokRWzJqQ/s320/CTZsZdEVAAAOMKd.jpg" width="212" /></a></div><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Experiments underway to&nbsp;<a href="http://www.npr.org/2016/01/01/461310525/a-physicist-dreams-of-catching-dark-matter-in-the-act">search for Dark Matter</a>. See Lisa Randall's new book: <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Dark-Matter-Dinosaurs-Astounding-Interconnectedness/dp/0062328476/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">Dark Energy and the Dinosaurs: The Astounding Interconnectedness of the Universe.</a></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">R</span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">esearchers believe that we could&nbsp;<a href="http://futurism.com/links/first-time-scientists-identify-genes-brain-linked-human-intelligence/">manipulate&nbsp;genetic human intelligence</a>&nbsp;and give human cognitive capabilities a boost, using a newly discovered network of genes directly associated with neuron and brain activity.</span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCX6b17PVsYBQ0ip5gyeme-Q">Crash Course</a>&nbsp;is a YouTube Channel that adds to the list of cool sites that explain things clearly and well.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Here’s an interesting site. “<a href="https://www.psychologytoday.com/blog/how-we-do-it">How We Do It</a>” by Robert Martin, MD covers a wide of fascinating topics having to do with human reproduction, including of course sex. For example most mammal females have two womb chambers and so do a few, rare women. Why do human males have no penis bone?&nbsp;&nbsp;Why do testicles have to “chill”?&nbsp;&nbsp;And can warming them serve as a male contraceptive? Why must childbirth be so challenging?&nbsp;&nbsp;Marin also has a book, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/How-We-Do-Evolution-Reproduction/dp/0465030157/?_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=contbrin-20">How We Do It: The Evolution and Future of Human Reproduction</a>.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">And finally... T<span style="color: #191919;">he nematode&nbsp;<i>Caenorhabditis elegans</i>, a worm species 1 millimeter long with a nervous system containing just 302 neurons, is the perfect organism to model, on our path to understanding how neuron based nervous systems function. So far, these models have (for example) successfully run a LEGO mindstorms robot.&nbsp;&nbsp;Now scientists&nbsp;<a href="http://www.kurzweilai.net/real-time-3-d-video-of-nematode-brains-links-neurons-with-motion-and-behavior?utm_source=KurzweilAI+Weekly+Newsletter&amp;utm_campaign=12958e4ec0-UA-946742-1&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_term=0_147a5a48c1-12958e4ec0-281972889">have observed record the activity of 77 neurons from the animal’s nervous system in action</a>, flashing in real time as the worm moves about.</span>&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;">And if you don't yet think we live in cool times... well we do.</span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;georgia&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: xx-small;">========= Addendum for you denialists =========</span></span></span><br /><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="font-family: &quot;georgia&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: xx-small;"><br /></span></span><span style="font-family: &quot;georgia&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: xx-small;">*You… are… science-hating morons.&nbsp; Worse, you are fanatics who threaten the lives of our children.
